<div id="review_1131645790" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1131645790" />
    <a title="Ikram" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17065991-ikram"><img alt="Ikram" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505599855p2/17065991.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1131645790?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ikram" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ikram" href="/user/show/17065991-ikram">Ikram</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17065991-ikram?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17065991-ikram?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17065991-ikram?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17065991-ikram?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17065991-ikram?shelf=smells-like-pain">smells-like-pain</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1131645790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14791250652089638227">4.5 stars.<br/><br/><b> My name is Ivy Westfall, and my mission is simple: to kill the president’s son—my soon-to-be husband—and return the Westfall family to power. </b><br/><br/>When I first read the blurb of this book I just thought AMAZING. Some books you just know for sure that you'll enjoy them merely because of the premise. <br/><br/>I have to say I wasn't disappointed with this book, even though I feel like it wasn't as good as it could've been but still, I had a great time reading it! Let me tell you a little more about th</span>
  <span id="freeText14791250652089638227" style="display:none">4.5 stars.<br><br><b> My name is Ivy Westfall, and my mission is simple: to kill the president’s son—my soon-to-be husband—and return the Westfall family to power. </b><br><br>When I first read the blurb of this book I just thought AMAZING. Some books you just know for sure that you'll enjoy them merely because of the premise. <br><br>I have to say I wasn't disappointed with this book, even though I feel like it wasn't as good as it could've been but still, I had a great time reading it! Let me tell you a little more about the story:<br><br>Ivy is the daughter of the founder (the losing side) of their community, and as a tradition, she's part of the many teenagers who must marry the boys of the other side in order to maintain peace. Because Ivy is special, the guy she's marrying is pretty special too. Its none other than the son's president, Bishop. Ivy doesn't care all about that because she only have one mission. And that's to kill Bishop, which should be easy because her father and sister have been filling her with hate for the president and his son for as long as she could remember. But when Bishop turns out to be the sweetest guy ever, it complicated things a bit for Ivy. <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426023608ra/13964052.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of the things I loved most about this book was that it made you think both morally and politically. I asked myself many times what would I have done if I were in her shoes. The line is thin between what's wrong and what's right in this novel and that's what made it so believable I think.<br><br>I thought I'd throw in some of my favorite quotes:<br><br><b>“You’re easy to read, Ivy, but the whole book of you is complicated.” <br><br>“He didn’t save me, though. He allowed me the freedom to save myself, which is the very best type of rescue.” <br><br>“But I want to be better than the lessons they taught me. I want my love to be greater that my hate, my mercy to be stronger than my vengeance.” <br><br>“Is it still manipulation if you know it's happening, but it works anyway?” <br><br>“Life is one sick joke after another, I'm discovering. Because it hardly seems fair that it should hurt so much to finally get exactly what I've been wishing for.”</b> <br><br>So this was not your typical YA book where the protagonist becomes a love sick puppy when she meets the love interest. No, Ivy HATED Bishop.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395706935ra/9033758.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> What if you spend your whole life hating someone but then relize they dont deserve your hate? What if your hate was misplaced? <br><br><b>“Is this who I am? A girl who will do anything for her family? A girl who will sacrifice an innocent boy to prove she’s not soft? I don’t know. I don’t know anything anymore.”</b><br><br>Let's talk about the Ivy/Bishop relationship for a moment. So these two characters were both extremely likable. I felt like they completed each other and were a great match. The romance developed slowly which made it justified and believable. It wasn't like one moment Ivy hated him and the next she was head over heals in love with him. <br> I have to admit though, the whole time I was reading their kissing scenes I was like:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426023608ra/13964053.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>DAT ENDING DOE!<br>I need to stop reading books with cliffhangers when the next book is not out yet because it's driving me crazy! <br><br>Overall I think that more people should read this book. In my opinion, it could appeal to a large variety of readers. <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14791250652089638227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jillian " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3101094-jillian"><img alt="Jillian " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504472383p2/3101094.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1113213488" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12506122001641194450">Disclaimer: I received a copy of this book from Entangled Teen Publishing in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/>OH. MY. GOD.<br/><br/>I don't have any coherent thoughts at this point but here are some appropriate gifs. Stay tuned for a review on my booktube channel!<br/><br/><a href='http://s102.photobucket.com/user/bookishandnerdy23/media/needadrink_zpsz8yw8r2y.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s102.photobucket.com/user/bookishandnerdy23/media/soulhurts_zps10oj2nls.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416734063ra/12050289.gif' alt=' photo soulhurts_zps10oj2nls.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s102.photobucket.com/user/bookishandnerdy23/media/tumblr_lo1g6tgcf41qafrh6_zpsszczg56s.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

<div id="review_1477440649" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1477440649" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1477440649?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=betrayal">betrayal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=marriage-of-convenience">marriage-of-convenience</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=library-loan">library-loan</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=hangin-on-a-cliff">hangin-on-a-cliff</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1477440649" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7246919192611058577">Okay.. I loved this. I didn't know what I was getting into when I requested this from my library, but I wasn't disappointed. It's dystopian YA--yes, this sub genre is as common as breathing--and while this sub genre is also hard to refresh with new and exciting ideas, I really liked the premise of this one and how it moved. <br/>Ivy Westfall is promised to Bishop Lattimer, the presidents son. I won't recap the history/synopsis because I want to highlight what I loved. She has a mission and that's to </span>
  <span id="freeText7246919192611058577" style="display:none">Okay.. I loved this. I didn't know what I was getting into when I requested this from my library, but I wasn't disappointed. It's dystopian YA--yes, this sub genre is as common as breathing--and while this sub genre is also hard to refresh with new and exciting ideas, I really liked the premise of this one and how it moved. <br />Ivy Westfall is promised to Bishop Lattimer, the presidents son. I won't recap the history/synopsis because I want to highlight what I loved. She has a mission and that's to murder Bishop and help the rebellion take over, which is led by her father. <br />The problem is, things aren't adding up for Ivy. Everything she's ever been told seems to be a half truth or not real at all. On top of it all, her feelings for Bishop are getting stronger and deeper, not exactly conducive for murder. Her sister, Callie, is reminding her of her mission while her dad is guilt tripping her. Douches all the way, those two.<br /><br />What I loved was how Ivy came into her arranged marriage thinking she knew what she had to do, But once in it, once she gets to know Bishop, she becomes conflicted. Seeing her battle it out in her head was my favorite part, mainly because she didn't waste time being stubborn. <br /><br />This didn't have any action, possibly surprising for dystopian YA, but it worked. I loved the pacing, the sweet romance and the psychological consequences of being raised to fulfill a mission but having to question its merit. <br />Bishop was sweet and sexy and kind and wonderful...just a great man. There was a scene between him and Ivy that involved a game of truth or dare, and I adored it. The sexual tension between them was palpable and really set the tone for their evolving relationship. <br />I'll mention there was little heat, some heavy making out and stuff and considering they're married, that might come across as odd. However, since they were strangers upon tying the knot, I thought it made sense. <br /><br />Of course things must come to a head and they did in the most dramatic of ways. I thought what Ivy did was commendable, but God, I felt sorry for her. The last 10% was very stressful and emotional. This ends on a big cliffy but I picked up the sequel which ends the series and I can't wait to jump right in! </span>
  <a data-text-id="7246919192611058577" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1064517877" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1064517877" />
    <a title="Rachel  (APCB Reviews)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12502667-rachel-apcb-reviews"><img alt="Rachel  (APCB Reviews)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468898958p2/12502667.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1064517877?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel  (APCB Reviews)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel  (APCB Reviews)" href="/user/show/12502667-rachel-apcb-reviews">Rachel  (APCB Reviews)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1064517877" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13900034242656326974">See the full review <a href='http://aperfectioncalledbooks.blogspot.com/2014/11/blog-tour-book-of-ivy-by-amy-engels.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>@ A Perfection Called Books</a><br/><br/>Things that I loved about this book:<br/><br/>1. The Plot<br/><br/>There are so many qualities of The Book of Ivy that make it so wonderful. It's definitely my favorite dystopian novel of the year. The concept is interesting and well-executed. There are twists and turns that you never see coming. There were slow moments, there were fast-paced moments, the pacing was great. I felt that everything happened for a reason. Every scene held some importance. There's tension a</span>
  <span id="freeText13900034242656326974" style="display:none">See the full review <a href="http://aperfectioncalledbooks.blogspot.com/2014/11/blog-tour-book-of-ivy-by-amy-engels.html" rel="nofollow noopener">@ A Perfection Called Books</a><br /><br />Things that I loved about this book:<br /><br />1. The Plot<br /><br />There are so many qualities of The Book of Ivy that make it so wonderful. It's definitely my favorite dystopian novel of the year. The concept is interesting and well-executed. There are twists and turns that you never see coming. There were slow moments, there were fast-paced moments, the pacing was great. I felt that everything happened for a reason. Every scene held some importance. There's tension and questioning throughout the book. The anxiety levels are high. We all want to know Will she do it? Is she going to kill him?<br /><br />2. The Writing<br /><br />Amy's writing is amazing!! She developed great characters and a great romance. Her world-building was stellar. She weaved the information in perfectly without it being an info-dumb yet not stretched too thin that we were confused. She was concise and descriptive and not overly so.<br /><br />3. The Feels<br /><br />I felt everything when I read this book. Anger, betrayal, bliss, upset, agony, shock, the whole spectrum. Amy plays with our hearts throughout this novel. She manages to pull out all the feels!! <br /><br />4. The Romance<br /><br />It's a slow burn. It's perfect. We see the romance actually grow and develop in this book. It's realistic and wonderful and I totally ship them!<br /><br />Overall I was very impressed with this book. It's definitely a new favorite of mine, I highly recommend it!</span>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alicia Batista (Addicted Readers)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alicia Batista (Addicted Readers)" href="/user/show/14564026-alicia-batista-addicted-readers">Alicia Batista (Addicted Readers)</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer907518960" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14240088084264898937"><br/><i> <b>4 Stars</b> </i><br/><br/>THE BOOK OF IVY was full of love, betrayals, murder plots, deception, and the courage to do what is in your heart, no matter the consequences...<br/><br/>I've had THE BOOK OF IVY on my radar for a while now, but since it sounded vaguely familiar to another book I read, ABERRANT, I was reluctant to pick it up. But my curiosity won me over and I finally decided to give THE BOOK OF IVY it's fair shot regardless of the similarities I thought they had. But I am pleasantly surprised to admit that was n</span>
  <span id="freeText14240088084264898937" style="display:none"><br /><i> <b>4 Stars</b> </i><br /><br />THE BOOK OF IVY was full of love, betrayals, murder plots, deception, and the courage to do what is in your heart, no matter the consequences...<br /><br />I've had THE BOOK OF IVY on my radar for a while now, but since it sounded vaguely familiar to another book I read, ABERRANT, I was reluctant to pick it up. But my curiosity won me over and I finally decided to give THE BOOK OF IVY it's fair shot regardless of the similarities I thought they had. But I am pleasantly surprised to admit that was not the case and the similarities were very minor, and it was definitely worth the read.<br /><br />THE BOOK OF IVY was very slow paced with hardly any action, but that was strangely okay with me. I still enjoyed the drama and suspense of it all. There were a lot of layers and plots and schemes and tons of betrayals that kept this story interesting enough even without the action and adventure. And the world-building was a little different then what I excepted, but still interesting enough. Though I would of liked to have more history on the war and conflict between the families, but I'm hoping we'll get more info in book two, THE REVOLUTION OF IVY.<br /><br /><i> <b>THE PLOT</b> </i><br /><br />After the war, Ivy's ancestors founded Westfall Community, a place that the people could rebuild and start anew. But their was disagreement about how to keep things up and running, and who should run them. The Westfall's and the Lattimer's went head to head for the position, and as fate would have it, the Lattimer's were the ones who seized control of Westfall Community. But instead of killing the rival family, they made the Westfall's the lowest citizens of their Community, and forced them to marry off their future children to the future Lattimer children, and thus seizing even more control of the Westfall's and the Community.<br /><br /><i> <b>And then the murder plot begins...</b> </i><br /><br />Ivy Westfall is on a mission, one that could change the world as they know it. One that could bring her family to their rightful place in power. One that could bring freedom back to their people. One that could save their women from marrying monsters. One that will turn her into, a murderer...<br /><br /><i> <b>For the mission she must complete is simple:</b> </i><br /><br /><i> <b>"Marry the enemy, make him trust you, find the codes and guns, wait for the order, execute on site."</b> </i><br /><br />Easy right? To save her people Ivy must kill the only person that might really want to save them all—Bishop Lattimer, the enemy and the presidents son, but also the love of Ivy's life... She must kill the man she's grown to love if she's to change their world...<br /><br />So to sum it all up, THE BOOK OF IVY was way more then I anticipated. I reveled in this story and the slow paced plot with strong characters and a slow burning romance that made me want to stay up late for just one more chapter!!<br /><br />Overall, THE BOOK OF IVY is definitely a must read for dystopian fans out there. It's not your gritty, face-paced, action-packed dystopia, so if that's what your looking for you won't find it here. But if you want a slow burning romance, with a slower pace plot, fleshed with rich developed characters, with spunk and determination, and a desire to set what's wrong right, and to avoid the dirtier methods to get it, then THE BOOK OF IVY is something I'm sure you'll enjoy. I am soooo eagerly waiting for book two, THE REVOLUTION OF IVY. I can't WAIT to see what happens next, because that ending was a KILLER!!!!<br /><br /><i> <b>NOTE: I received a eARC from Entangled for reviewing purposes! All opinions express are my own and are not influenced in any way!</b> </i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14240088084264898937" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CLOAPk2RL0x9Uw6Z7qlnyG5lKCBahoKbRzxbMkgVd20WLY23LsS8mM5f2km3WKPyuzj0Wla+wI5kVjt3YUo/hw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/39931607-the-book-of-ivy">Quotes from The Book of Ivy</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
